Aaron tolerates the lower temperature without protest, which is itself developmental progress; the prior pattern would have been to tighten through pursuit. He waits. He answers when called. He does not push. When Miles re-extends, Aaron does not over-respond. The dyad recalibrates at a slightly more guarded but more honest equilibrium.

---

## 5. THE CLONE / ULTIMATUM PERIMETER

During the broader Clone Saga / Ultimatum crisis affecting Miles directly, Aaron's role is **peripheral and protective**. He is not operationally inserted into the conflict — he has neither the powers nor the gear in current loadout to be useful in a fight involving multiple superhuman Miles-variants and Selim/Ultimatum-tier opposition — but he is **available**, geographically and emotionally, in a way the prior Aaron was not. He provides logistics. He provides a non-Jefferson adult presence for Miles to decompress around. He provides, in a small but documented way, **a safe room** — his apartment functions as a tertiary refuge for Miles during the period, after the family brownstone and the girlfriend's apartment are compromised. This is, again, the architectural payoff of the fixed-address decision. He made himself locatable so that Miles would have a place to go.

His read on the Selim threat, when he weighs in, is tactical-uncle rather than vigilante: he assesses the man as a manipulator first and a fighter second, and counsels Miles to attack the **information** rather than the body. This is consistent with his lifetime cognitive style — surfaces and seams — applied generously rather than predatorily.

---

## 6. RELATIONAL CURRENT STATE

**With Miles.** Stable, post-disclosure equilibrium. Weekly contact, frequently more. Miles drops by the apartment without warning, which Aaron permits and visibly enjoys (the second chair at the table is in regular use). They watch sports. They cook badly. They do not — and this is important — train together; Aaron has explicitly stepped out of the combat-mentor role, recognizing that it was the wedge through which his prior pattern operated. He counsels, when asked, on city-navigation, on people-reading, on tradecraft applicable to the non-violent parts of Miles's double life. He has become, against all prior trajectory, the **uncle Miles actually needed in adolescence and is finally getting in late adolescence/early adulthood**. The relationship is the single largest asset on his current ledger and he knows it.

**With Jefferson.** Cool, formal, intermittently civil. The brothers are not reconciled. They are in **détente**, mediated entirely through Rio and through Miles. Jefferson tolerates Aaron's presence in family contexts (holidays, milestones) but does not seek him out and does not relax around him. Aaron, for his part, does not push. He has begun — in the most recent appearances — making small, plausibly-deniable gestures of repair: showing up on time, leaving early, not drinking at family events, not arguing when contradicted. The slow work of being a non-threat to his brother's household. There is no evidence the détente will warm in the near term and considerable evidence Aaron has accepted this. The addressee of his adult life has refused the letter and Aaron has, finally, stopped re-mailing it.

**With Rio Morales.** Notably warmer than with Jefferson. Rio is the conduit through which most family information flows to and from Aaron. She is courteous, watchful, and has demonstrably forgiven more than her husband has. Aaron treats her with a deference bordering on courtliness — he is on his best behavior in her presence in a way that is not calculation but gratitude.

**With Miles's peer group.** Aaron has minimal direct contact with Miles's superhuman cohort and prefers it that way. He has met Ganke once or twice in a context that read as "the uncle dropping something off" rather than integration. He does not socialize with Miles's romantic partner beyond civility. This is by design: he understands that any deeper integration into Miles's external life is exposure-risk for the boy and reputation-risk for himself, and he has chosen restraint.

**With prior criminal network.** Largely severed, with maintained back-channels. He is no longer working with the Scorpion-tier operators he used to subcontract from. He has, however, retained communications with a small number of fence-and-information assets — not for active use, but as **intelligence on himself**: if his name surfaces in the underworld he wants to know before Miles does. This is the residual operator's hygiene.

**With law enforcement.** Not an active subject of investigation, to inference. He has not, in the post-resurrection window, generated the kind of incident that puts him back on a board. His name persists in older files. He moves as a man who assumes a baseline of passive surveillance and does nothing actively to confirm it.

---

## 7. THE GEAR QUESTION

The Prowler suit and its associated technology are the most ambiguous element of his current operational footprint. The honest read of the available evidence:

The gear **exists**, in his possession, in his apartment, under the tarp at the back of the workspace. He has not destroyed it. He has not sold it. He has not surrendered it. He has, by every indication, **maintained** it — the gauntlets that killed him in another life are cleaned, repaired, and serviceable. This is the largest single piece of contrary evidence to a clean-reform reading.

The defensible interpretation: Aaron Davis has not put the suit down because he does not believe the world will let him. He has rebuilt his life around the bet that he can stay out of it, but he is not naive enough to bet his nephew's safety on the wager. The gear is **insurance**, not vocation. He has worn it, in the recent period, in exactly the situations the file would predict: when Miles or the family was under direct threat and conventional channels were inadequate. He has not worn it for a job. The distinction matters and the file should record it as the operative one.

The undefensible interpretation, which must also be entered: a thief does not keep his tools clean unless some part of him is keeping the door open. Aaron may not himself know which interpretation is correct. The maintained gauntlets are the material expression of the unresolved part of the formulation.

---

## 8. SOMATIC AND PSYCHOLOGICAL CURRENT STATE

**Body.** Age-appropriate decline from operational peak, well-managed. He has thickened slightly through the middle, lost a step of pure speed, retained the grip strength and the close-quarters reflexes. The old injuries register in cold weather — he favors the right shoulder, rolls the neck more often than he used to, sits down with the small exhalation of a man whose knees have begun to keep their own books. He carries himself, in public, in the lightly-folded posture he has used his whole adult life to occupy less visual space than his frame would otherwise claim. In private, with Miles, the posture opens — shoulders back, longer stride, easier laugh.

**Grooming.** Beard maintained, trimmed weekly, not styled. Hair short. Clothes are quiet — dark jackets, dark jeans, soft-soled shoes, nothing branded loudly. He owns one good suit. He owns no jewelry of consequence. He wears a watch, mechanical, that he winds himself; this is the only personal vanity on the public record.

**Affect.** More available than at any prior point in the file. He laughs more readily, sits in silence more comfortably, tolerates being looked at without deflecting. The chronic vigilance has not vanished — it will not — but it has decompressed. He can be in a room without scanning it for the first thirty seconds, which a man with his history cannot have done in decades.

**Internal weather.** Inferentially: a settled, low-grade sadness about Jefferson that he has stopped fighting; a working pride in the rideshare income that he would never name as pride; a daily, almost ritual gratitude for Miles's presence that he expresses only through availability; and an unspoken, hard-edged awareness that the second chance is conditional and that he is one bad night from losing it. This last is not paranoia; it is accurate. He is living, deliberately, **inside the conditionality**, which is the most adult thing he has ever done.

---

## 9. CURRENT THREAT POSTURE

**Threats to him.** Residual underworld memory; the Assessor's network or its successors; any operator who learns of his Miles-connection and decides to use him as a vector; old enemies of the Prowler identity who do not know or care that he has stepped down. The fixed address that is the foundation of his reform is also his single largest tactical vulnerability. He has accepted the trade.

**Threats from him.** Low under current conditions. Moderate-to-high under conditions that activate his shame structure or threaten Miles directly. The pressure points enumerated in the personality section remain live. Hand him a situation involving children, trafficking, or a coercer who thinks they own him, and he becomes operationally unpredictable in the same way the file has always recorded — overriding self-interest, gear coming out from under the tarp, the old competence going to work in service of something other than a payday.

**Trajectory.** Positive, fragile, **load-bearing on a single relationship**. The reform is real and the reform is contingent. If Miles is in his life, Aaron Davis is one of the most usefully reformed criminals in the boroughs. If Miles is removed from his life — by estrangement, by violence, by the natural drift of an adult nephew building his own world — the file would expect regression, not necessarily to crime per se but to the affective desert that crime was always the medication for.

---

## 10. WHERE HE IS NOW

He is in the apartment. The radiator is on. There is coffee in the pot from this morning that he will pour cold over ice if the afternoon gets warm. The phone is on the counter, face up, in case Miles calls. The keys for the sedan are on the hook by the door. The tarp at the back of the workspace has not been moved this week. He has a fare scheduled in forty minutes — a regular, an older woman who goes to dialysis on Tuesdays and Thursdays and tips in cash. He will be on time. He will help her with the door. He will not play music. He will drive carefully. He will come home. He will, in the evening, watch a game he does not care about and wait, without admitting he is waiting, to see if the boy calls.

This is the current state. It is more life than he had any right to expect and he is, by every available indicator, **trying to deserve it**.


## Medical History

# UATU ANALYTICAL FILE: AARON DAVIS / THE PROWLER
## SECTION 2 — MEDICAL HISTORY

*Compiled from longitudinal behavioral observation across both continuities (Ultimate-1610 and post–Secret Wars 616). No medical records survive in admissible form — subject's criminal status precludes a continuous clinical chart — so the file is reconstructed from on-panel somatic evidence, behavioral inference, equipment-correlated injury patterns, and the testimony of family contact. The medical picture of Aaron Davis is the medical picture of a man who has spent thirty years declining to see doctors.*

---

### 2.1 CONSTITUTIONAL BASELINE

**Phenotype.** Adult male, Black, mid-thirties to early forties across the published window. Height approximately 5'11"–6'0". Build: lean-mesomorphic, low body-fat percentage, musculature distributed for sustained climbing and burst sprint rather than for display — the somatotype of a working burglar, not a gymnasium project. Reach long for his height. Hand size large, with the thickened palmar and finger-pad architecture associated with chronic grip loading (parkour, rope, edged-tool use). No tattoos of identifiable affiliation; one or two small unobtrusive marks consistent with informal/jailhouse work, location-protected by sleeve. Hair kept close-cropped or shaved — operationally hygienic, low DNA-shed surface, also a tell of someone who minimizes time in front of mirrors.

**Congenital / developmental.** No documented inherited conditions. The Davis brothers' family medical history is opaque on-page; what can be inferred from Jefferson's own profile (cardiovascular discipline, no chronic illness pattern) suggests a constitutionally robust line. No evidence of childhood asthma, diabetes, sickle-trait clinical expression, or neurological abnormality. He is, structurally, a healthy man who has spent his adult life undoing that health.

**Dentition.** Intact, asymmetrically maintained. Visible wear pattern on the right canine and lateral incisor consistent with chronic clenching under stress and possible nocturnal bruxism — a somatic stress signature corroborated by the affect-regulation profile (Section 3). No evident professional dental care in the Ultimate window; some catch-up work inferable in the 616 reform arc when the subject is briefly insured through gig-economy paperwork.

**Vision and hearing.** Both functionally above baseline, neither superhuman. Operational reliance on optics in the Prowler gear suggests low-light vision compensated rather than innate; he wears the goggles even when ambient light would not require them, indicating a learned dependency. Hearing intact but with the high-frequency notch characteristic of repeated unmuffled close-range gunfire and the percussive output of his own gauntlets — early-onset noise-induced hearing loss, subclinical, presents as the slight lean-in and the reflexive turn of the better ear toward the speaker in noisy rooms.

---

### 2.2 CHILDHOOD AND ADOLESCENT MEDICAL RECORD (RECONSTRUCTED)

The Davis brothers grew up in an environment whose ambient violence is referenced obliquely in both continuities and made explicit in the 616 family-history flashbacks. Aaron's pre-adult medical record is therefore inferred rather than documented, and inferred dark.

**Probable injury pattern, ages 8–18.** Multiple unhealed or imperfectly healed minor fractures — knuckles, nasal bridge, possibly a metacarpal or two on the dominant hand. The slight rightward deviation of his nose in clean profile shots is consistent with at least one untreated nasal fracture in adolescence. Knuckle architecture across both hands suggests repeated boxer's-fracture-type insults healed by splinting-of-convenience rather than reduction. The faint scar at the left eyebrow is the kind a ring catches on or a curb produces — neither set under sterile conditions.

**Probable absence of well-child care.** No vaccination gaps documented but none confirmed; the subject's later willingness to enter biohazard environments (Oscorp lab break-in, Brooklyn warehouse settings with rodent exposure) without observable prophylactic concern suggests either complete immunization confidence or — more likely — a learned indifference to infectious risk that is itself diagnostic.

**Adolescent musculoskeletal loading.** The shoulder mobility, hip turnover, and ankle resilience he displays in his prime climbing sequences are not adult-acquired. He has been moving up the sides of buildings, fences, fire escapes, and stairwells since before his growth plates closed. This produces the specific architecture visible in his late-thirties body: dense forearm and grip development, pronounced latissimus and serratus engagement, and the slightly forward shoulder carriage of someone whose pectoral and anterior deltoid chains overdeveloped relative to the posterior chain in early adolescence and were never corrected.

**Psychological impact of the developmental medical history.** Most of his early injuries were sustained in conditions where to seek care would have been to invite questions — from a parent, a school nurse, a juvenile officer, eventually a probation system. He learned, before he was old enough to articulate it, that the body's repair is something one supervises personally and quietly. This produced the adult who treats his own injuries on a kitchen table with a needle and a bottle of something, who knows which over-the-counter combinations will hold a fever down through a night job, and who experiences a hospital waiting room as a hostile interrogation environment rather than a place of care. The medical avoidance is not stoicism — it is a conditioned response.

---

### 2.3 THE FOUNDATIONAL EVENT

The robbery-with-death that ended the Davis brothers' partnership and Aaron's relationship with Jefferson is the file's hinge. Medically, this is when the subject's somatic vigilance baseline resets upward and stays up. There is no on-record injury from that night for Aaron, which is itself notable — the man who walked out of that room intact was the man whose body kept the score for the next twenty years.

The hypervigilance, the foreshortened sleep architecture, the eating-on-the-move pattern, the room-scan-on-entry behavior — all of it dates, on the inferential timeline, to that night and the months immediately following it. He has been running an elevated sympathetic-nervous-system baseline since his early twenties. The cardiovascular cost of two decades of low-grade fight-or-flight tone is real, and shows in subtle signs: the resting jaw tension, the faint tremor visible in his off-hand during prolonged stillness, the unexplained sweating in temperate rooms when a topic approaches Jefferson.

---

### 2.4 OCCUPATIONAL MORBIDITY: THE CRIMINAL CAREER

Across roughly fifteen years of professional B&E and crew work prior to the published window, and through the published window itself, the subject accumulates a soft-tissue and orthopedic injury load consistent with a career second-story man and gear-augmented operator.

**Documented and inferred orthopedic insults.**
- **Hands.** Multiple healed metacarpal fractures, particularly the fourth and fifth on the right. Chronic mild osteoarthritis beginning in the thumb CMC joints from edged-tool use and gauntlet engagement. The subject favors his right hand for fine work, his left for grip.
- **Wrists.** Repetitive strain consistent with the Prowler gauntlet's recoil and load-bearing function. The wrists are the joint most likely to fail him first; he stretches them unconsciously between actions, a tell that should be coded.
- **Shoulders.** Bilateral rotator cuff tendinopathy, low-grade, chronic, untreated. Visible as the slight catch in his draw motion when reaching above shoulder height for sustained loads. Probable partial labral tear on the right from a fall or a wrench he never had imaged.
- **Knees.** Bilateral patellar tendinopathy from repeated drop-landings off building edges and fire escapes. The subject lands quietly because he has learned to, but his knees pay the rent. By the 616 reform window he is sitting down more carefully than a man his age should need to.
- **Lower back.** Chronic lumbar paraspinal tension and probable L4–L5 disc wear from years of carrying weight in a torso-held pack while moving asymmetrically across vertical surfaces. Reads in the small adjustments he makes when standing from low chairs.
- **Ankles.** Both demonstrate the proprioceptive scarring of multiple sprains; he rolls them less than he used to because his foot-placement is more deliberate, not because the joints are sound.

**Soft-tissue and integumentary record.** Numerous small scars across the forearms and shins from edged tools, climbing hardware, and ventilation ductwork. A burn-pattern scar on the medial right forearm, narrow and linear, consistent with a soldering iron used in his own gear-modification work. At least one healed laceration on the lateral thigh deep enough to have warranted sutures it did not receive; the resulting scar tissue contracts in cold weather and produces a slight, intermittent limp the subject masks with cadence variation. Knuckle scarring on both hands consistent with bare-fist and gloved-fist contact across years.

**Specific event injuries from the published record.**
- **Scorpion confrontations (Ultimate).** Repeated blunt-force trauma. The beating he takes in the Scorpion arc would have produced, in a civilian, an emergency-room visit for likely concussion, rib contusions, and probable hemothorax workup. Aaron walks it off, sleeps it off, and is operational again within days. Concussion history is almost certainly substantial and unscored. There is no record of him having ever been formally evaluated for traumatic brain injury, and the cumulative cognitive cost — slight word-finding hesitation under fatigue, occasional repetition of phrasing across days — is consistent with low-grade chronic TBI sequelae that have not yet, in the published window, crossed clinical threshold.
- **Gauntlet electrical injury, terminal (Ultimate continuity).** The fatal event: his own malfunctioning gauntlets discharge catastrophically, producing combined high-voltage electrical and thermal burn injury sufficient to cause death. The mechanism is consistent with arc-flash event at close range — entry and exit pathway likely through the upper limbs and across the thorax, with cardiac arrhythmia as the proximate cause of death and full-thickness burns as the visible signature. The Ultimate-arc death is, importantly, a death by his own tools — the medical record's final entry in that continuity is the literalization of a theme that has been somatic the whole time: the instruments of his survival are the instruments of his harm.
- **616 reform-arc injuries.** The Assessor coercion and the trafficking-adjacent confrontations produce a different injury register — closer to interrogation-grade than combat-grade. Restraint marks, the shock of being out-leveraged, and at least one beating administered as message rather than as fight. He recovers. He also, for the first time on record, accepts brief medical contact from a clinic willing to ask no questions — a small but real behavioral shift that is the medical correlate of the reform arc.

---

### 2.5 EQUIPMENT-DEPENDENT MEDICAL PROFILE

Aaron Davis has no superhuman physiology. He is a baseline human whose operational ceiling is set entirely by his gear — Prowler suit, clawed gauntlets, optics, projectile and edged armaments, climbing assist, occasional aerosolized incapacitants. This produces a specific medical syndrome that conventional clinical literature does not have a name for but that surveils cleanly across the file: **his survival capacity is exosomatic, and the exosoma has demonstrably tried to kill him.**

**Direct medical consequences of gear use.**
- **Cutaneous and dermatologic.** Chronic pressure-points and chafing where the suit interfaces with the body, particularly at the shoulders, hips, and the medial thighs. Recurrent folliculitis in occluded areas. Mild contact dermatitis from prolonged wear, managed by tolerance rather than treatment.
- **Thermoregulatory load.** The suit traps heat. Long jobs produce significant fluid loss; he hydrates aggressively before and after but rarely during, which is why he eats salty food on the way to a job and drinks heavily on the way home in a manner that would alarm a sports-medicine clinician.
- **Inhalation exposures.** Years of break-ins through ductwork, demolition-adjacent industrial sites, and aerosol-using engagements produce a probable mild reactive airway pattern. He coughs in the morning more than he used to. He does not smoke; the cough is the building dust talking back.
- **Auditory.** As noted above, the gauntlet discharges and the close-range gunfire of his crew encounters have notched his hearing.
- **Radiation / unusual exposures.** The Oscorp break-in that sets the entire Miles arc in motion involved a non-trivial exposure window in a laboratory environment of demonstrated biohazard. Aaron carried the spider out; whatever else he carried out is unscored. He shows no overt sequelae, but the exposure is on the record.

**Psychological consequences of the equipment dependency.** The subject's relationship to his own tools is latently adversarial. He maintains the gear obsessively — clean, lubricate, test, recalibrate — in a ritual whose stress-signature exceeds what the engineering requires. The maintenance is propitiation. He half-knows the gauntlets can turn on him, has on at least one occasion (Ultimate, terminal) been right, and on every subsequent occasion (616) is operating with that knowledge as ballast. The man who polishes his claws on the workbench at 3 a.m. is not performing diligence. He is negotiating with the part of himself that the tools represent.

---

### 2.6 SUBSTANCE USE PROFILE

**Alcohol.** Social-to-moderate, consistent across both continuities. Bourbon and beer the principal vehicles. No documented blackout history; no observed dependency pattern; tolerance high in a way that suggests sustained moderate use rather than binge architecture. He drinks to come down off a job, not to numb a life. The post-job drink is functionally medicinal — parasympathetic re-entry after sympathetic peak — and this is one of the few self-regulation strategies he has that is not the work itself.

**Tobacco.** Negligible. Occasional social cigarette in specific company. Not a smoker; lung function intact apart from the dust cough.

**Cannabis.** Inferable occasional recreational use, not operational. He does not work impaired. He may sleep impaired.

**Stimulants, opioids, cocaine, methamphetamine.** No on-record use. The absence is diagnostic in itself: a man with this risk profile, this pain load, this ambient stress baseline, and this access to product who is not using is exercising deliberate restraint, and the restraint is craft-protective. He has watched stimulants destroy operators and opioids destroy crews, and he has decided he will not be that file. The decision is mature and unsentimental.

**Performance-enhancing or self-medicating use.** Likely intermittent over-the-counter NSAID use at doses that, sustained, would warrant a gastrointestinal workup he is not getting. Probable caffeine dependency, expressed through a specific morning ritual the surveillance file would document precisely (one strong coffee, prepared the same way, drunk in the same posture at the same window). Possible periodic use of off-prescription muscle relaxants acquired through gray-market channels for post-job recovery.

**Psychological reading of the substance profile.** The notable absence here is the absence of self-medication for shame. A man carrying Aaron's load of fraternal disinheritance and instrumental-uncle guilt is statistically expected to chemically manage it; he does not. The work is the medication. The job is the substance. This is part of what makes the criminal pattern so resistant — it is functioning as his anxiolytic, his antidepressant, his attachment substitute, and his self-esteem regulator simultaneously, and no pharmaceutical intervention will outcompete it. The 616 reform arc is, in pharmacological terms, an attempt at polypharmacy substitution (driving, family contact, ordinary daytime structure) for a single agent (the work) that has been doing all the work. Substitutions of this kind notoriously relapse, and his do.

---

### 2.7 SLEEP, NUTRITION, AND SOMATIC STRESS MARKERS

**Sleep.** Light, fragmented, vigilance-shaped. The subject sleeps with the door in his line of sight, an exit identified, a weapon within reach. Total sleep duration likely 5–6 hours on a good night, less on operational ones. Sleep latency low — he can drop quickly when conditions are right — but arousal threshold also low; small sounds bring him to full alertness within seconds. The architecture is consistent with chronic sympathetic dominance: short, shallow, easily fractured. Daytime micro-sleeps in safe environments (a car, a couch in Miles's apartment, a porch) are the subject's compensatory mechanism. He is most relaxed asleep in spaces Miles has implicitly secured for him, which is its own diagnostic note.

**Nutrition.** Caloric intake adequate, structure poor. Eats on the move, eats late, eats fast. Has the metabolic forgiveness of someone who runs his body hard daily; this will end in his mid-forties if it has not already begun. Sodium load high. Vegetable intake low except as garnish. In the 616 reform window, demonstrable improvement under family-meal exposure — Rio's cooking, sit-down dinners at the Davis-Morales table — is one of the few unambiguously positive medical interventions in the file.

**Cortisol-load behavioral signature.** Chronic vigilance produces the cluster: clenched jaw, shallow upper-chest breathing pattern at rest, slight tremor in stillness, sweat response disproportionate to ambient temperature, mild but persistent gastrointestinal complaints he does not articulate, intermittent tension-pattern headaches. He carries his stress in the trapezius and the masseter. Watch the jawline on still frames — when it sets, he is somewhere far away from the conversation.

**Cardiovascular.** Resting heart rate likely low (the climbing keeps the engine tuned) but variability poor. The man's cardiovascular system is conditioned but not regulated — capacity high, recovery sluggish, ANS tone stuck high. He is at elevated medium-term risk for hypertension and stress-mediated cardiac events that no clinician has had the opportunity to flag.

---

### 2.8 TRANSFORMATIONS, ALTERATIONS, AND CONTINUITY-DEATH

**Death and restoration.** The Ultimate-continuity death by gauntlet electrocution is, in the medical file, the maximum-severity entry. The post–*Secret Wars* restoration to 616 continuity is not a clinical event he experiences — it is a metaphysical reset — but its phenomenology for him is the lived sense of a second chance whose origin he cannot articulate. The 616 Aaron does not remember dying. He carries, however, the affective residue of a man who at some level knows the gauntlets have already killed him once, and this residue is the engine of the reform arc more than any conscious decision is.

**No documented superhuman transformations.** Aaron Davis is not powered. He is not infected, mutated, irradiated to effect, or symbiotically bonded on the record. He remains, across both continuities, a baseline human whose remarkable capacity is entirely a function of training, gear, and nerve. This is medically relevant because it means he ages on a normal human curve, accumulates injury on a normal human curve, and will degrade on a normal human curve — and he knows it. The actuarial awareness is the secret of the reform arc.

**No surgical record.** No documented elective procedures, no documented emergency surgical interventions on the published record. Given the injury load, this is not because he has not needed any — it is because he has not received any. There is, almost certainly, hardware-grade orthopedic damage in this man's body that is being managed by avoidance rather than repair.

---

### 2.9 INTEGRATED PSYCHOLOGICAL IMPACT OF THE MEDICAL HISTORY

The medical file and the psychological file are, in Aaron Davis's case, the same file written in different alphabets.

The childhood injury pattern taught him that bodies are managed privately. The career injury pattern taught him that pain is a tax. The equipment relationship taught him that the things that keep him alive will eventually try to kill him. The substance restraint pattern taught him that he can hold a hard line when he decides to, which is the same capacity the 616 reform arc requires. The chronic sympathetic dominance taught him that safety is something other people have, not something he inhabits — except, intermittently, in the specific physical proximity of his nephew, which is the one place his nervous system measurably downshifts.

He has never been in a medical setting where someone with authority looked at his body and named what they saw. The closest he has come to that experience, in either continuity, is the moment Miles looks at him after a bad night and says some version of *you don't have to do this anymore.* The clinical relationship Aaron Davis has, functionally, is with his nephew. The diagnosis is *uncle*. The prescription is *stay*.

The Ultimate file closes with the gauntlets. The 616 file is still open. The somatic record will, in either case, end the way it has tended the whole time — quietly, privately, without consultation, and with the tools in the room.


## Somatic Atlas

# UATU ANALYTICAL FILE: AARON DAVIS / THE PROWLER
## Section 6 — SOMATIC ATLAS

*The body as logged across the published behavioral record. Where the panel evidence is direct, it is treated as observation; where it is implicit in posture, framing, or repeated staging, it is treated as inference with the somatic logic shown. This is the granular bodily file: the inventory a long-running physical-surveillance package would compile across years of static and motion capture.*

---

### 6.1 Build, Frame, and Standing Carriage

Aaron presents as a tall, lean-muscled Black man in his mid-to-late thirties, body composition tilted toward functional rather than display strength — the wiry, shoulder-and-back-dominant musculature of a climber and a carry-load athlete rather than the chest-and-arm front-loading of a weightlifter. The body is built by the job: pulling himself up, holding himself flat against vertical surfaces, dropping his weight silently. Visible forearm definition; trapezius development consistent with rope and ledge work; calves and hip flexors recruited heavily, visible when he is in suit. Bodyfat low but not stripped; he eats enough.

**Standing baseline (calm).** Weight slightly back on the heels, hips loose, one foot habitually a half-step forward of the other — never fully squared to a conversational partner. The asymmetric stance is the resting form; perfectly square stance is a tell that he has decided the conversation matters and he is performing attention. Shoulders sit a fraction low and rolled back; he does not slouch but he does not military-posture either. Hands tend to live below the waist — in pockets, hooked in belt loops, resting on a hip, holding a cup, holding a phone — almost never crossed at the chest. Chest-crossing is a stress posture for him, not a baseline.

**Standing under mild stress.** The forward foot advances a few inches more. The chin drops about a centimeter. Hands come up out of pockets and find an object — keys, phone, a glass — to occupy. He smiles more, not less.

**Standing under threat.** Stance widens almost imperceptibly; weight redistributes forward of the heels onto the midfoot; the rear knee unlocks. He looks the same to a casual observer and entirely different to a trained one. The hands come fully empty and stay open at thigh level. He does not raise his guard. He raises the floor.

**Standing in intimacy (with Miles, predominantly).** The asymmetry collapses. He squares up. He gets physically lower — leans on counters, sits on stoops, drops into a crouch to be at the kid's height even when the kid has long since stopped being short. The lowering is the most consistent intimacy-marker in his entire physical repertoire.

---

### 6.2 Gait

**Walking baseline.** Long stride, low vertical bounce, soft heel-strike rolling forward through the midfoot — the trained-quiet walk of a working burglar that has bled permanently into civilian life. He cannot un-walk it. On a hardwood floor, on metal stairs, on the catwalks above a job, the cadence is the same: 105–110 steps per minute, even pressure, the audible signature minimized. Arm swing is restrained — elbows close to the ribs, hands relaxed, the shoulders carrying very little of the motion.

**Walking stressed.** Pace lengthens by perhaps ten percent; cadence drops slightly. He covers more ground per step and makes more noise doing it. The arm swing opens up. He looks, to the uninitiated, more relaxed when stressed — because the trained quietness costs effort and the effort sheds first.

**Walking in pursuit / on a job.** The cadence inverts: shorter steps, higher cadence, weight pitched forward, head still. He moves like a man who has rehearsed not casting a shadow. He hugs walls without touching them — habitually keeps a ten-to-twelve-inch standoff that allows full lateral evasion. He clears doorways with a shoulder-first pivot rather than a face-first peek.

**Running.** Economical, mid-stride, arms cycling close. He is not a sprinter; he is a distance-and-obstacle runner, and he conserves. On rooftops in the suit he runs with a slight forward lean and a habit of clipping his foot strike on the parapet edges to convert horizontal momentum into vault energy. He does not vocalize when running. No grunting, no breath-counting. Breath stays in the nose as long as possible.

---

### 6.3 The Hands

The single most expressive territory on his body, and the one a surveillance package would film most.

**At rest.** Long fingers, palmar calluses concentrated on the heel of the hand and the pads of the second and third fingers — the wear pattern of a man who grips bars, ledges, and tool handles, not one who throws punches first. The knuckles are scarred but not deformed; he has been in fights, but the fights have not been his primary medium. The nails are kept short, square-filed, scrupulously clean — a grooming standard inconsistent with the rest of his presentation, and therefore diagnostic. Dirty nails would tell on him at a job; he has internalized the discipline so thoroughly that the cleanliness persists when he is not working. A surveillance file would note the manicure as the most reliable identity marker available short of biometrics.

**Gestural vocabulary in conversation.** He talks with his hands in a low, mid-torso arc — palms-up, palms-out, fingers spread, a lot of small open shapes that read as transparency. The gestures are pedagogically clear and rhetorically warm; they are also a learned set he uses to lower a counterpart's guard. With Miles in mentor mode the hands come into the conversation a lot — sketching diagrams in air, miming grip work, pantomiming a sequence. With strangers in transactional mode the hands stay lower and more still; he conserves.

**Tics and self-touch.**
- Right thumb running along the pad of the right index finger — a small, continuous rolling motion that surfaces when he is thinking through an angle. Inaudible, almost invisible, and present in virtually every panel where he is calculating.
- Pinching the bridge of his own nose between thumb and index when shame surfaces (highly characteristic of the 616 reform-arc beats; rare in Ultimate).
- The back of the hand brushed across the jawline — a grooming-derivative gesture that appears when he is deflecting; it buys him a half-second of face-cover while he composes the next line.
- Tapping the side of a closed fist twice against a thigh or a tabletop before standing up to leave. A self-cue. It marks decision-points.
- With keys, coins, or any small metal object in pocket: a quiet thumb-and-finger sorting, never rattled aloud. Even his fidgets are noise-disciplined.

**Hands under threat.** They go still and empty. The fidgets stop. Both hands hang open at his sides, fingers slightly curled, the way a man stands who has decided what he is going to do and is waiting for the geometry to allow it. The stillness is the warning. People who know him read it; people who do not, do not.

**Hands in suit.** The clawed gauntlets change his proprioception measurably: his reach effectively extends two to three inches and he learns, over years, to compute it without thinking. Out of suit he occasionally over-reaches for objects — a residual calibration error from too many hours in the gear. A surveillance team would clock the over-reach as a Prowler-positive tell long before it clocked anything else.

---

### 6.4 Face: Microexpression and Habitual Set

**Resting face.** Mouth neutral with a faint upward set at the corners — the engineered half-smile of a man who has decided that "approachable" is a tactical baseline. The eyes do not match the mouth. The eyes scan. The disjunction is constant and, once seen, unmissable: the face below the eyes performs warmth; the eyes do work.

**Eyes.** Scan pattern is room-centric, not face-centric. Entering an unfamiliar space he runs a sweep — exits, elevated positions, anyone armed, anyone watching him — before he locks onto whoever he came to see. The sweep takes about two seconds and he has practiced making it look like he is just looking around. Pupil behavior is normal-reactive; he does not have the dead-flat eye of a deep psychopathic register, and a careful observer can see real emotion arrive in the eyes seconds before it reaches the mouth. With Miles the scan shortens dramatically and the eye-contact extends; he holds Miles's gaze for full conversational beats in a way he does with no one else.

**Smile vocabulary.**
- *The work smile.* Wide, teeth-showing, asymmetrical (left side rises faster). Deployed for marks, civilians, anyone he is reading. Lasts a fraction longer than a spontaneous smile and resolves cleanly back to neutral.
- *The kid smile.* Smaller, closer-mouthed, slower to arrive and slower to leave, crinkling the outer corners of the eyes. Reserved for Miles. Appears once per interaction at minimum and is the most reliable behavioral evidence on file that the attachment is real.
- *The job smile.* A private, almost-smirk that surfaces when something on a job goes elegantly — a clean alarm bypass, a satisfying drop. The smile of craft pride. He does not perform it; it arrives.
- *The cornered smile.* A tight, closed-mouth flicker that appears under coercion or accusation. It is a stress signal that observers misread as composure. It is not composure.

**Jaw.** Strong baseline jaw; under stress the masseter visibly tightens — a quiet but reliable tell. He grinds at night (inferred from waking-jaw tension and from the somatic load profile); a dentist would find the wear.

**Brow.** Mobile, expressive, used heavily in mentor mode (the raised-brow questioning beat with Miles — *"and what would you do?"*). Stress flattens it. Threat flattens it further. The brow is the first part of the face to leave when the body switches modes.

**Nostril and breath.** Nasal breathing dominant. Audible exhale through the nose is an irritation marker — short, sharp, dismissive — and one of the few honest signals he lets escape. Under threat the breath cycle lengthens and quiets to near-silence; he has trained this.

---

### 6.5 Voice and Speech Somatics

Mid-baritone, lightly resonant, with the rhythmic and lexical signature of Brooklyn. Speech is paced, never rushed; he uses pauses as punctuation and is comfortable in silence in a way most of his interlocutors are not. The pause is itself a tactic — it pushes the other speaker into the gap.

**Volume profile.** He is a quiet talker by default. Forces the listener to lean in. Volume rises only in performative warmth (greeting Miles), in mock outrage (humor under pressure), and very rarely in actual anger, where the voice paradoxically *drops* — going lower and quieter as the affective stakes climb. The drop-into-quiet is his most dangerous register.

**Lexical tics.**
- Frequent use of *"little man"* and *"nephew"* as address terms for Miles — endearments deployed slightly too often, with the rhythm of a man making sure the relational frame stays named aloud.
- *"Look —"* as a sentence-opener when he is about to lie or to manage.
- *"Trust me"* — used sparingly, but its appearance correlates strongly with him about to be untrustworthy. A tell he does not know he has.
- Code-switches register fluently — street-fluid with Miles or with operators in his world, neutralized and articulate with marks and with civilians he needs to put at ease.

**Laughter.** Two distinct laughs. The performed one — a quick three-beat *ha-ha-ha* with mouth-open display — is deployed at jokes that are not funny, to lubricate interaction. The real one — quieter, lower in the chest, with a closed-mouth shudder — is rare and almost always provoked by Miles. The real laugh ends with him shaking his head, eyes briefly closed.

---

### 6.6 Grooming and Self-Presentation

Beard maintained at a uniform short length — neither stubble nor full beard but the deliberate middle. Lineup at the cheek and the neck kept crisp; he goes to a barber on a regular cycle and would notice if the cycle slipped. Hair short, low-fade, similar discipline. Scalp clean. Skin well-maintained — he uses moisturizer (inferred from consistent finish and the climate-neutral skin condition across panels).

The wardrobe choices map to a deliberate signaling system: leather jacket as outerwear default, layered over fitted tees and henleys; dark denim; clean low-profile sneakers or boots, never showy. Nothing in the kit has a visible logo larger than a stitched tag. The aesthetic reads as *expensive-but-not-traceable* — every piece quality, nothing that would be picked out of a witness description as distinct. This is operational dressing rendered as personal style; he has been doing it so long he no longer experiences it as a choice.

Accessories are scrupulously minimal. One watch, functional, kept on the left wrist. No rings (anything on the hands fouls climbing and signals identifiers). No chains visible. Wallet flat, in the front pocket — not the back, which is both a pickpocket-defense and a sitting-comfort decision. Phone in left front pocket; right pocket reserved for the dominant hand.

He smells of clean laundry, restrained cologne (something cedar-and-skin, not loud), and, faintly and persistently, the metallic note of his gear-room — solvent, lubricant, machined metal. The Prowler bleeds through the civilian envelope.

---

### 6.7 Sleep Architecture

Light sleeper, broken cycles, very short sleep latency in a secured environment and very long latency in an unsecured one. Estimated total sleep five to six hours on a working week, with occasional ten-hour collapse-recovery sleeps on the back end of jobs. He does not nap socially; he naps tactically, in chairs, in vehicles, in fifteen-to-thirty-minute increments, and wakes without disorientation.

**Pre-sleep ritual.** Doors checked twice. Phone face-down on the nightstand. Weapon (or, in the 616 reform arc, the legal pepper spray that substitutes for it) within arm's reach. Lights out before screen-off, never the reverse. He sleeps on his side, dominant arm tucked under the pillow, the hand on or near the weapon. Sleeps in clothes more often than is healthy — boxers and a tee at minimum, never fully nude, even alone.

**Sleep position.** Predominantly left-side fetal, knees drawn up, oriented toward the bedroom door. He has not slept with his back to a door in his adult life. In hotel rooms or unfamiliar safehouses the bed gets dragged or the body re-oriented until the door is in his field of view on waking.

**Wake pattern.** Eyes open before the rest of him moves. A full ten-to-fifteen-second motionless assessment — sound, light, smell — before he sits up. The wake-scan is the morning version of the room-entry scan. A long-term partner would learn it; he has not had a long-term partner, which is itself a datum.

**Disturbed sleep.** Bruxism (jaw-grinding, inferred). Restless lower-leg movement in the second half of the night, consistent with a chronically activated sympathetic baseline. Nightmares not directly documented but inferable from the post-Jefferson-confrontation beats where he is shown awake and dressed at unsociable hours. He does not remember dreams aloud.

---

### 6.8 Eating Patterns

Eats on the move, eats fast, eats functionally. Calorie intake is high relative to his frame because the work burns hard; macro split skews toward protein and complex carbohydrate, with a consistent secondary thread of greasy comfort food (a slice, a halal cart plate, a diner breakfast). He has a small number of trusted regular spots — the kind of New York food infrastructure a man builds when he eats out five nights a week and wants to be remembered enough to be greeted and ignored enough not to be questioned.

**Pace.** Fast eater. Plates clear in ten to twelve minutes. He does not linger over food alone; he lingers over food with Miles. Meals with the nephew last three times as long as any other meal in his life.

**Coffee.** Daily, black, regular, no ceremony. Carried in a paper cup more often than drunk in a chair. The cup is a hand-occupier as much as a beverage.

**Alcohol.** Social, controlled, beer or brown liquor neat. Two-drink ceiling in public; the discipline is operational, not moral. He needs his reaction time and he knows it. Drinks more at home alone occasionally — the data point a careful observer would note is that the alone-drinking covaries with Jefferson-proximate stress.

**Water.** Underhydrated by athletic standards. He does not carry a water bottle. A small somatic vanity-blind-spot.

**Food and intimacy.** Cooking does not appear in his repertoire. He feeds Miles by buying — slices, takeout, the shared meal as gift. The transaction *is* the affection. In 616, the Uber-driver arc forces a more domestic eating pattern that he is still learning; he is shown more often with groceries than was previously visible, and the awkwardness of the unpacking is itself part of the reform.

---

### 6.9 Sexual and Intimate Somatics

The on-panel sexual record is thin by design — Bendis and Ahmed both keep this off-stage — but a surveillance file would infer the following from what *is* shown.

He reads as conventionally heterosexual, with a low-disclosure dating pattern: short-duration relationships, partners outside the family's knowledge, no cohabitation documented. The relational style maps to the dismissing-avoidant template established in the psychological section — high charm at intake, declining intimacy gradient, exits managed cleanly. He does not appear to seek serious partnership and may experience the prospect as threat-adjacent (it would require domestic stability of the kind his work cannot support, and disclosure of the kind his identity cannot survive).

Physical affection vocabulary outside the sexual register: he hugs with one arm, the dominant hand free; the embrace is brief, firm, terminated by a back-slap. The slap is the exit punctuation. With Miles the hug gets the second arm and lingers a beat longer; this is one of the few unmistakable somatic intimacy upgrades he gives anyone. Hand on the back of Miles's neck, hand on Miles's shoulder, knuckle-light to the jaw — a tactile vocabulary of fond men's-physicality that he reserves almost exclusively for the nephew.

He does not flinch from touch initiated by trusted others but does not initiate it broadly. Handshakes are firm, single-pump, eye-contact-met; he releases first. He has trained the release.

---

### 6.10 The Suit as Second Body

Time in the Prowler suit reorganizes his somatic profile measurably. Posture shifts forward — the claws and the shoulder armor pull the centre of mass; he compensates with a slight pelvic tuck and a more flexed knee at standing rest. Gait shortens and the footfall lightens further; the suit's grip system encourages a digitigrade-leaning approach to vertical surfaces and a soft, almost feline approach to horizontal ones. He breathes through the mask in a measured four-count he does not use out of suit.

The voice changes in the suit — modulated by the mask, but also by him: a register lower, the affect flatter, the lexical playfulness stripped. The Prowler is not a separate personality; he is the same man with the warmth disabled. The disabling is itself a tell. He cannot be charming in the gear, and he does not try.

Coming out of the suit, there is a five-to-ten-minute decompression window in which his civilian affect is muted and his movements are more economical than baseline. A surveillance officer with a long lens would learn to recognize the post-suit window: the quietness, the longer pauses, the eyes still scanning at job-tempo. He returns to baseline through a specific sequence — gear off, hands washed, water, sit down, exhale — that functions as the descent ritual. Interrupting the ritual makes him irritable in a way nothing else does.

---

### 6.11 State Transitions: The Master Table

A consolidated map of how the body shifts across the four operational states.

**Calm.** Asymmetric stance, hands low and occupied, mid-baritone speech, mouth-corner-upturned face, room-scan completed and parked, breath nasal and unhurried, the rolling-thumb fidget present, the work smile available, the kid smile latent.

**Mild Stress.** Hands rise to object-holding height, talk increases, work smile increases in frequency and decreases in duration, masseter visibly engages, breath audibly exhales through the nose, "look —" lexical opener appears, decision-tap on thigh foreshadows departure.

**Threat.** Stance widens and weight comes forward, hands empty and open, voice drops in pitch and volume, brow flattens, fidgets cease, eyes lock and stop scanning (target acquired), breath quiets to inaudibility, the cornered smile flickers and resolves to flat. The most dangerous version of him is the most still version of him.

**Intimacy (Miles-coded almost exclusively).** Stance squares and lowers, the kid smile arrives and stays, eye-contact extends across full conversational beats, two-armed hugs with held duration, hand on neck or shoulder, real laugh in the chest, meals stretched, the lexical *little man / nephew* deployed as relational tether, the room-scan suspended for the first time in any given day.

---

### 6.12 Aging and Wear

Across the publication record his body shows the cumulative cost: a small persistent hitch in the right hip on cold mornings (consistent with an old rooftop landing); a slight favoring of the left shoulder when reaching overhead (rotator wear from years of climbing); a thin scar along the right forearm and another at the left collarbone, both visible only when shirtless; the burn-and-electrical injury record of the Ultimate timeline never accrued in 616, where his skin is correspondingly cleaner. The hands age fastest — the calluses thicken, a knuckle stiffens, the manicure discipline persists. He has the body of a man who has used himself hard and maintained himself carefully, and who knows, in a way he does not say aloud, exactly how many more years the body will let him do the work.

The somatic file closes on that knowledge. Every habit catalogued above is, in the last analysis, a strategy by the body to keep the man alive long enough to figure out what to do with the one relationship he has not yet ruined.


## Attachment & Relational Patterns

# UATU ANALYTICAL FILE — AARON DAVIS / THE PROWLER
## Section 7: Attachment & Relational Patterns

---

### 7.1 Origin of the Attachment Architecture

To map Aaron Davis's relational system you must first map the room he learned love in, and that room had two doors: the one his mother walked through and the one his brother stood in. The Davis household record — assembled across the Ultimate flashback fragments and the more developed 616 family material in Ahmed's run — is consistent on a small set of facts. The brothers grew up in proximity to violence that was both ambient (neighborhood) and intimate (the family's own peripheral involvement in it). Their father's record is the one neither brother volunteers; what they volunteer is each other. In every flashback panel that establishes the boys young, **Jefferson is the smaller figure looking up and Aaron is the larger figure looking out** — the older brother in the doorway, scanning the street, deciding what comes in.

This is the originating attachment template and it never leaves him. Aaron's first organized relational role was **protector-by-vigilance**, and the entire adult repertoire — the room-scan on entry, the over-reading of strangers, the gift-bringing, the operational tempo control — is that eight-year-old's job description grown up. He learned that love means watching the door, and he never learned that love also means sitting down at the table once the door is shut. Sitting down is the part he never got to.

The rupture event — the joint robbery in young adulthood that ends with someone dead or dying and the brothers split forever — is the **second** formative event, but it is not, properly read, the origin of Aaron's avoidance. It is the confirmation of a hypothesis he had already been carrying: that the people you watch the door for will, when given the chance, treat you as the threat outside the door. Jefferson's excommunication is so absolute — Miles raised not knowing Aaron exists, not by oversight but by **deliberate, sustained erasure across a decade-plus** — that it functions in Aaron's psyche less as rejection and more as ontological annulment. His brother did not stop loving him; his brother undid him. From that point forward, every relational move Aaron makes is shaped by the unspoken assumption that he is provisionally real to other people, and could be unmade again at any moment.

This produces the attachment signature on file: **dismissing-avoidant operationally, preoccupied-anxious in the one channel he keeps open.** It is not a contradiction. It is the only viable adaptation when your foundational object proved that closeness can be retroactively voided.

---

### 7.2 How He Bonds

Aaron's bonding sequence is a recognizable, repeating, four-stage protocol, observable across every meaningful relationship in the file — with Miles, with the women glimpsed at the edges of his Ultimate-era life, with his criminal collaborators in their early-warm phase, and even, latterly, with the regulars on his 616-era driving route.

**Stage one: the read.** Within seconds of meeting someone he intends to make use of, or someone he begins to feel something toward, Aaron performs a comprehensive scan — body language, tells, what they want, what they fear, what they're hiding. This is not predatory in intent (though it is in mechanism); it is how he has always assessed whether a person is safe. The scan is automatic and continuous. Even with Miles, even years in, he is still scanning. The scan is also how he loves: paying attention this hard to someone is the only intimacy he was trained for.

**Stage two: the offering.** Aaron does not declare; he provides. He shows up with the thing the other person didn't ask for but wanted — sneakers for Miles, a tip about a job for a peer, a ride for a stranger in 616. The offering is calibrated to the read and is the closest he gets to verbal declaration. He almost never says *I see you*. He hands you the object that proves he did.

**Stage three: the shared activity.** Bonds consolidate, for Aaron, through co-operation in the literal sense — operating together. With Miles it is the rooftop training sessions and, calamitously, the jobs. With his criminal peers it is the work. With the women in his life it is shared night-economy activity — going somewhere late, doing something interesting. He cannot sit across a table and talk about his feelings; he can do something next to you that lets you read him in motion. This is his equivalent of disclosure.

**Stage four: the test.** This is the diagnostic stage, the one that distinguishes him from a true psychopath and from a healthy attacher both. At some point Aaron will do something that risks the relationship — usually a controlled bit of leverage, a small betrayal of confidence, an ask he knows is too large. He is not aware he is testing; he reads it as opportunism. But the **function** is to find out whether the bond will survive him being himself. If it survives, he relaxes incrementally. If it doesn't, he confirms his prior. The test is structured to be passable by people with high tolerance and impossible to pass cleanly, which is why most of his bonds eventually fray on this exact stage. Miles passes it repeatedly. Jefferson, in Aaron's memory, did not, and the test is partly an unconscious re-staging aimed at finding someone who will.

---

### 7.3 How He Distrusts

Aaron's distrust does not present as suspicion. It presents as **charm with the temperature off**. Watch the eyes in the Bendis panels where he is dealing with someone he has decided not to fully credit — the Scorpion, an Oscorp middleman, the Assessor's intermediaries: the mouth keeps working, the joke lands, the body stays loose, but the gaze runs three-quarter-flat. He has functionally two registers of attention — full-beam (for marks, for Miles, for active threats, for anything he might love or rob, which are categorically similar in his nervous system) and matte (for everyone he has decided is a transaction). The transition between registers is fast and the subject usually does not notice.

He does not voice distrust; he routes around it. If Aaron stops asking you about your life, he has demoted you. If he stops bringing you objects, he has written you off. If he goes quiet on the comms during a job, he has already begun planning the contingency in which you are not in the room. He almost never confronts a betrayal directly because confrontation requires admitting he expected better, which is an admission of attachment, which is an admission of exposure. He prefers to **vanish from a relationship**, leaving the other party uncertain whether anything happened at all. This is the avoidant signature in its purest form.

The exception, again, is Miles. With Miles, distrust produces the opposite signature: pursuit, intrusion, escalating contact. When he begins to feel Miles slipping — the Ultimate arc documents this precisely — he tightens, gets in closer, calls more, offers more, finally threatens. He cannot vanish from the one bond that matters because vanishing would be Jefferson's move and Jefferson's move is the one he cannot make. So he stays, and stays badly, and breaks it from the inside.

---

### 7.4 How He Betrays

Aaron's betrayals are not impulsive. This is one of the most important entries in the file and it bears on the diagnostic question of whether the antisocial-features formulation hardens or softens with time. Aaron does not betray in the moment. He betrays **after a documented internal negotiation** in which he weighs the relationship against the operational gain and persuades himself that the leverage is the lesser evil because it preserves the contact. The Ultimate-era extortion of Miles is the type case: he frames coercion to himself as **insurance against losing the nephew**, because if Miles disengages voluntarily Aaron has no recourse, but if Miles is leashed by the secret then the contact is structurally guaranteed. This is monstrous and it is also, recognizably, love-logic deformed by avoidant attachment.

The betrayals therefore follow a consistent topology:

- They are **proximate to anxiety about losing the relationship**, not to anger about the relationship.
- They are **leverage-based** rather than violent or expressive — he weaponizes information, access, or implication, not fists.
- They are **immediately rationalized** as care or instruction ("I'm teaching him real-world skills"; "this is how he survives this life").
- They are **remembered with shame** rather than forgotten, which is the part that disqualifies the psychopathic reading.
- They **escalate when met with resistance** rather than retracting, because retraction would require admitting the original move was a betrayal, which would require admitting he is the thing his brother said he was.

He does not betray strangers; he uses them, which he does not classify the same way. The betrayal category is reserved, in his own internal taxonomy, for the people who had a claim on him. There are not many such people. The category is dangerous mostly to the people inside it.

---

### 7.5 How He Repairs

The repair record is thin in Ultimate and the central spine of the 616 arc. In Ultimate, Aaron dies before repair becomes available; the gauntlet death reads, on second pass, as a man who has burned his only bond and has stopped flinching at the prospect of his own end. In 616 he gets the chance and the file finally accumulates repair behavior worth describing.

**Aaron repairs slowly, non-verbally, and through demonstration.** He does not apologize cleanly — when he attempts the verbal apology to Miles in the Ahmed run it comes out hedged, deflective, half-jokey, true underneath but armored on the surface. What he does instead is **show up repeatedly without asking for anything**, which is the inverse of his bonding-stage-two offering. The reformed-uncle behavior is precisely calibrated to undo the extortion era: where once he came with gifts that obliged a return, now he comes with presence that asks for nothing. The asymmetry is the apology.

He also repairs through **third-party demonstration**: in the 616 arc he is observably gentler with people who are not Miles — driving fares, neighbors, the trafficked civilians he intervenes for — and Miles is meant to see it and does. Aaron is showing his nephew the man he could have been, in the medium he can speak in, which is action toward strangers rather than speech toward kin.

He does not repair with Jefferson, in either continuity, in any sustained way. The Jefferson-rupture is the one he cannot work on because working on it would require sitting in a room with his brother and naming what happened, and naming what happened would require either of them to take the larger share of the blame, which neither will. Their on-page interactions are brief, armored, and end as soon as politeness permits. This is the unrepaired hinge of the entire psyche.

---

### 7.6 Intimacy and Dependency

Aaron's intimacy capacity is **narrow-channel, high-bandwidth**. He cannot do mild intimacy with many people; he can do intense intimacy with one or two. The Ultimate and 616 records both show him circulating among acquaintances — bartenders, fences, drivers, peripheral lovers — none of whom get past the matte register. The full-beam channel is reserved.

**Romantic and sexual record.** The file is genuinely thin here, which is itself diagnostic. Aaron is shown in proximity to women — implied partners, brief scenes — but no sustained romantic relationship is documented across the published material. This is consistent with the avoidant architecture: a man who learned that the foundational sibling bond could be retroactively annulled does not invest in pair-bonding, because pair-bonding requires sustained mutual exposure of the kind that, in his template, ends in erasure. He likely conducts an active but compartmented sexual life — episodic, non-cohabiting, ending before either party can issue a claim. The absence of a documented long-term partner is not evidence of incapacity; it is evidence of deliberate operational hygiene applied to the domain that scares him most.

**Dependency.** Aaron does not allow himself to be visibly dependent on anyone. He pays cash, owes no favors he cannot retire quickly, lives in spaces he can leave on short notice, owns tools he services himself. The Ultimate-era over-reliance on the Prowler gear is the exception that proves the rule, and it kills him: the one thing he let himself depend on (the suit) was the one thing that turned. After that, in 616, watch how he behaves toward the new gear — warier, more diagnostic, less identified-with. He learned the lesson the only way he learns lessons, which is by being hurt by the object of his trust.

The hidden dependency, the one he cannot acknowledge, is on Miles. Miles is the only person whose continued existence in his life Aaron cannot tolerate the loss of, and the entire 616 reform arc is, beneath its surface, a long quiet negotiation with that dependency — trying to organize his life such that the dependency does not destroy the nephew the way it nearly did in Ultimate.

---

### 7.7 The Repeated Template

Across every relationship in the file, with variations in intensity, Aaron runs the same loop. It is worth writing out as the loop, because once you see it once you see it everywhere in the record.

1. **Scan and select.** He identifies someone whose seams he can read, who has something he wants — material, social, or affective.
2. **Offer and engage.** He provides the calibrated gift or service, establishes the shared-activity bond, performs the warm-uncle / cool-operator register at full beam.
3. **Consolidate through co-operation.** The relationship deepens through doing things together rather than saying things to each other.
4. **Sense the precarity.** At some point — sooner with non-kin, later with kin — he registers (often unconsciously) that the relationship could end and that he has no insurance against it ending.
5. **Test and / or leverage.** He performs the small betrayal, the ask-too-large, the introduction of a transactional element into what had been (to the other party) a non-transactional bond.
6. **Rationalize.** He frames the leverage as care, instruction, or pragmatic necessity.
7. **Escalate if resisted; vanish if matte; pursue if kin.** The relationship now bifurcates based on category. Matte relationships end with him not returning calls. Kin relationships intensify into coercion.
8. **Collapse or repair.** In Ultimate, all loops end in collapse. In 616, the Miles loop, uniquely, enters a repair phase characterized by silent demonstration and the active suppression of stages 5 and 6 when they try to recur.

The loop is the man. It is not a character flaw to be fixed; it is the operating system his developmental environment installed, and the only meaningful intervention in the published record is the **conscious arrest of stages 5 and 6 in the one relationship that matters most**, which Aaron achieves intermittently in 616 and which constitutes, by the standards of this kind of structure, a major and hard-won clinical accomplishment.

---

### 7.8 Specific Relational Cartography

**Jefferson Davis.** The unrepaired hinge. Aaron's posture toward his brother is one of pre-emptive defense disguised as casualness — he addresses Jefferson with the affected lightness of someone who has rehearsed not caring. The body tightens when Jefferson enters a scene; the joking accelerates; the eyes go matte in a way they do for no one else, because with Jefferson the full-beam channel was burned out long ago and the matte register is a scar tissue substitute. Aaron will never initiate the conversation that would repair this. If repair ever comes it will come because Jefferson initiates it, and Aaron will accept it with such over-controlled gratitude that the scene will be almost unwatchable.

**Miles Morales.** The full-beam channel. The displaced object of the brother-bond and the test case for whether Aaron's loop can be arrested. Every behavior toward Miles is overdetermined — uncle-love, brother-substitute, redemption-vehicle, mirror — and Aaron cannot disentangle the strands. The 616 arc's central achievement is that he stops trying to disentangle them and just tries to behave well within the tangle.

**Criminal peers (Scorpion, the Ultimate-era ecosystem).** Matte register, transactional. He extends provisional respect to operators of comparable craft and withdraws it instantly from sloppy ones. He betrays this category without significant internal cost because they were never in the kin frame to begin with. The Scorpion confrontations are about ego (the craftsman insulted by the brute) rather than attachment.

**Coercers (the Assessor, handlers).** Hatred-coded. Aaron tolerates beatings, jobs gone wrong, and material losses far better than he tolerates being managed. Anyone who attempts to own him triggers a deep characterological resistance — likely because being owned is structurally similar to being un-owned by Jefferson, both being conditions in which his existence is at another's discretion. He will betray a coercer at the first viable opportunity and feel righteous about it.

**Civilians and bystanders.** Indifferent baseline, with a sharp protective spike for children, the trafficked, and the visibly defenseless. This is the moral floor of the man and it is real. The 616 arc weaponizes it deliberately — when Aaron sees a trafficking operation, the loop disarms entirely and he becomes operationally unpredictable in ways that override self-interest. This is the closest thing in the file to evidence of an internalized ethic rather than a contingent code, and it is the strongest argument for the rehabilitative reading.

**Strangers in the 616 driving-economy life.** A new and diagnostically interesting category. The fares, the regulars, the neighbors — Aaron is rehearsing, in this category, a kind of low-stakes warmth he never previously practiced. It is not intimate but it is not matte either; it is a third register he is constructing in middle age, the warm-acquaintance channel, and it represents real characterological growth. He is building, late, the broad shallow surface of casual connection that most people build in their twenties and that he could not build then because he was busy watching the door.

---

### 7.9 Summary Diagnostic

Aaron Davis attaches the way someone walks on a leg that was broken young and set wrong — functionally, with adaptation, with pain that no longer announces itself, and with a permanent altered gait that anyone trained to see it can read across a room. He bonds through vigilance and provision, distrusts through temperature drop rather than withdrawal of contact, betrays through anxiety-driven leverage that he rationalizes as care, and repairs — when he repairs at all — through silent sustained demonstration rather than speech. He maintains one full-beam channel and rations the rest of the world to the matte register. He cannot do pair-bonding and has organized his life to not need to. He cannot speak to his brother and has organized his life around the nephew who is the brother's proxy. The relational template is consistent, legible, and — uniquely in the 616 arc — partially modifiable, on the single channel that matters, through the costly daily work of refusing to run stages five and six of his own loop. That refusal, sustained, is the entire content of his redemption. It is not visible as heroism. It is visible as a man not doing the thing he wants to do, on a Tuesday, in a car, with his nephew in the passenger seat, and not saying why.


## Defenses & Compensatory Mechanisms

# UATU ANALYTICAL FILE: AARON DAVIS / THE PROWLER
## Section 7 — Defenses & Compensatory Mechanisms

*Cross-referenced against Sections 3 (Psychological) and 4 (Psychiatric). This section enumerates the full defensive architecture: every mechanism evidenced in the canonical record, ranked by developmental primitiveness per the Vaillant hierarchy (mature → neurotic → immature → primitive), with operational behavior, behavioral tells, failure modes, and the somatic micro-signatures by which each can be identified on observation. Compensatory mechanisms — both adaptive (positive) and pathological (negative) — follow.*

---

### 7.1 The Architectural Overview

Aaron Davis's defensive system is unusual among career criminals in that it is **stratified rather than collapsed**. Most lifelong offenders, by the age band where Aaron is first observed (mid-thirties, *Ultimate Comics Spider-Man* #1), have flattened their defensive repertoire to a small set of primitive operations — projection, acting out, denial — applied broadly and crudely. Aaron has not. He retains, alongside the primitive material, a working layer of **mature defenses** (sublimation, humor, anticipation) and a substantial **neurotic layer** (rationalization, intellectualization, reaction formation, displacement). The result is a man who can, under sufficient pressure, deploy the entire developmental ladder within a single encounter — sublimating into craft on entry, intellectualizing the score in mid-job, splitting the target halfway through, acting out on exit, and rationalizing the whole sequence over a drink afterward.

This stratification is the engine of his ambiguity. Pure primitives would make him a low-functioning offender easy to predict; pure neurotic-mature would make him Jefferson. He is jagged because his defenses are jagged, and the jaggedness reflects an interrupted developmental arc: someone whose internal architecture matured normally until the rupture event with Jefferson, after which integration stalled and the primitive layers — quarantined but not metabolized — remained available as fallback whenever attachment heat rose past tolerance.

The diagnostic implication: under low affective load he reads as a high-functioning charming professional. Under attachment activation specifically (Miles in a room, Jefferson mentioned), the strata destabilize and primitive material breaks surface within seconds. **Defense quality in Aaron is inversely proportional to relational proximity.** With strangers he is sophisticated. With kin he regresses.

---

### 7.2 Mature Defenses

#### 7.2.1 Sublimation

The most evident and most load-bearing of his mature operations. Aaron's craft — the planning, the entries, the elegant in-and-out — is a **direct sublimation of aggression and disinheritance into culturally legible (if illegal) skill**. The aggression that, in his brother, was metabolized into the disciplined defensiveness of straight life is in Aaron metabolized into offense as artistry. He takes pride in *clean* jobs. He scorns smash-and-grab operators (visible in his contempt for the Scorpion's blunt methodology). He talks about heists the way a chef talks about a service.

*Behavioral tells:* He narrates jobs in the past tense with a craftsman's specificity — entry vector, alarm topology, the second the guard pivots. He becomes more, not less, articulate when describing technical sequences. The voice drops slightly into a teaching register. Hand movement increases: he traces routes in air.

*Failure mode:* Sublimation requires a channel. When the channel is blocked — equipment confiscation, surveillance saturation, the 616-era straight-job period — the sublimated aggression has nowhere to go and seeps into the relational sphere instead, where it presents as irritability, restlessness, and the gravitational drift back toward a job.

#### 7.2.2 Humor

Aaron's humor is **tactical** — deployed at the precise moment another person would disclose, escalate, or freeze. He uses it to manage interpersonal distance (jokes with Miles to skim over the asymmetry of their power), to defuse confrontation (the half-smile when Jefferson's name lands), and to occupy social space without filling it with self. It is a mature defense because the humor is genuinely funny and other-directed; it is also a control mechanism because the humor *terminates* topics he does not wish to continue.

*Behavioral tells:* The corner-of-mouth quirk that precedes a deflection. A particular short exhaled laugh — single syllable, not a full laugh — used as a punctuation mark to close a subject. Eye contact is *maintained* through humor (atypical for him; he is otherwise a glancer), because the humor *is* the contact substitute.

*Failure mode:* Under sufficient stress the humor brittles into sarcasm, which is no longer mature — it has slid down into passive-aggression and signals the defensive line is collapsing.

#### 7.2.3 Anticipation

He is constitutionally a planner. The defensive function of anticipation is to convert anxiety into preparation — to render the unknown into a sequence of contingencies so that affect never reaches threshold because the situation has been pre-disarmed.
